[1m[7m%[27m[1m[0m                                                                                ]7;file://Anmols-MacBook-Pro.local/Users/anmolsaini/Wright_State_University/CEG_4350[0m[27m[24m[Janmolsaini@Anmols-MacBook-Pro CEG_4350 % [K[?2004hmman chf mod[?2004l
[?1049h[?1h=CHMOD(1)                     General Commands Manual                    CHMOD(1)

[1mNAME[0m
     [1mchmod[0m ‚Äì change file modes or Access Control Lists

[1mSYNOPSIS[0m
     [1mchmod[0m [[1m-fhv[0m] [[1m-R[0m [[1m-H[0m | [1m-L[0m | [1m-P[0m]] [4mmode[24m [4mfile[24m [4m...[24m
     [1mchmod[0m [[1m-fhv[0m] [[1m-R[0m [[1m-H[0m | [1m-L[0m | [1m-P[0m]] [-a | +a | =a] [4mACE[24m [4mfile[24m [4m...[24m
     [1mchmod[0m [[1m-fhv[0m] [[1m-R[0m [[1m-H[0m | [1m-L[0m | [1m-P[0m]] [[1m-E[0m] [4mfile[24m [4m...[24m
     [1mchmod[0m [[1m-fhv[0m] [[1m-R[0m [[1m-H[0m | [1m-L[0m | [1m-P[0m]] [[1m-C[0m] [4mfile[24m [4m...[24m
     [1mchmod[0m [[1m-fhv[0m] [[1m-R[0m [[1m-H[0m | [1m-L[0m | [1m-P[0m]] [[1m-N[0m] [4mfile[24m [4m...[24m

[1mDESCRIPTION[0m
     The [1mchmod[0m utility modifies the file mode bits of the listed files as
     specified by the [4mmode[24m operand. It may also be used to modify the Access
     Control Lists (ACLs) associated with the listed files.

     The generic options are as follows:

     [1m-f[0m      Do not display a diagnostic message if [1mchmod[0m could not modify the
             mode for [4mfile[24m, nor modify the exit status to reflect such failures.

     [1m-H[0m      If the [1m-R[0m option is specified, symbolic links on the command line
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             are followed and hence unaffected by the command.  (Symbolic links
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             encountered during tree traversal are not followed.)
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-h[0m      If the file is a symbolic link, change the mode of the link itself
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             rather than the file that the link points to.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-L[0m      If the [1m-R[0m option is specified, all symbolic links are followed.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-P[0m      If the [1m-R[0m option is specified, no symbolic links are followed.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             This is the default.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-R[0m      Change the modes of the file hierarchies rooted in the files,
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             instead of just the files themselves.  Beware of unintentionally
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             matching the ‚Äú[4m..[24m‚Äù hard link to the parent directory when using
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM     The [1mchmod[0m utility modifies the file mode bits of the listed files as
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM[1mDESCRIPTION[0m
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             instead of just the files themselves.  Beware of unintentionally
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             matching the ‚Äú[4m..[24m‚Äù hard link to the parent directory when using
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             wildcards like ‚Äú.*‚Äù.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-v[0m      Cause [1mchmod[0m to be verbose, showing filenames as the mode is
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             modified.  If the [1m-v[0m flag is specified more than once, the old and
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             new modes of the file will also be printed, in both octal and
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             symbolic notation.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The [1m-H[0m, [1m-L[0m and [1m-P[0m options are ignored unless the [1m-R[0m option is specified.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     In addition, these options override each other and the command's actions
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     are determined by the last one specified.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     If [1mchmod[0m receives a SIGINFO signal (see the [1mstatus[0m argument for stty(1)),
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     then the current filename as well as the old and new modes are displayed.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     Only the owner of a file or the super-user is permitted to change the mode
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     of a file.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[1mEXIT[0m [1mSTATUS[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The [1mchmod[0m utility exits¬†0 on success, and¬†>0 if an error occurs.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[1mMODES[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     Modes may be absolute or symbolic.  An absolute mode is an octal number
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     constructed from the sum of one or more of the following values:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           4000    (the setuid bit).  Executable files with this bit set will
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   run with effective uid set to the uid of the file owner.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Directories with this bit set will force all files and sub-
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   directories created in them to be owned by the directory
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   owner and not by the uid of the creating process, if the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   underlying file system supports this feature: see chmod(2)
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   and the [1msuiddir[0m option to mount(8).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           2000    (the setgid bit).  Executable files with this bit set will
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   run with effective gid set to the gid of the file owner.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           1000    (the sticky bit).  See chmod(2) and sticky(7).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0400    Allow read by owner.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0200    Allow write by owner.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0100    For files, allow execution by owner.  For directories, allow
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   the owner to search in the directory.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0040    Allow read by group members.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0020    Allow write by group members.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0010    For files, allow execution by group members.  For
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   directories, allow group members to search in the directory.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0004    Allow read by others.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0002    Allow write by others.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0001    For files, allow execution by others.  For directories allow
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   others to search in the directory.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     For example, the absolute mode that permits read, write and execute by the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     owner, read and execute by group members, read and execute by others, and
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     no set-uid or set-gid behaviour is 755 (400+200+100+040+010+004+001).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The symbolic mode is described by the following grammar:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM                   underlying file system supports this feature: see chmod(2)
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM                   owner and not by the uid of the creating process, if the
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM                   directories created in them to be owned by the directory
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM                   Directories with this bit set will force all files and sub-
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM                   run with effective uid set to the uid of the file owner.
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM           4000    (the setuid bit).  Executable files with this bit set will
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM     constructed from the sum of one or more of the following values:
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM     Modes may be absolute or symbolic.  An absolute mode is an octal number
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM[1mMODES[0m
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0002    Allow write by others.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           0001    For files, allow execution by others.  For directories allow
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   others to search in the directory.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[HM     constructed from the sum of one or more of the following values:
[24;1H[K:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   others to search in the directory.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     For example, the absolute mode that permits read, write and execute by the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     owner, read and execute by group members, read and execute by others, and
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     no set-uid or set-gid behaviour is 755 (400+200+100+040+010+004+001).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The symbolic mode is described by the following grammar:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           mode         ::= clause [, clause ...]
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           clause       ::= [who ...] [action ...] action
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           action       ::= op [perm ...]
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           who          ::= a | u | g | o
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           op           ::= + | - | =
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           perm         ::= r | s | t | w | x | X | u | g | o
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The [4mwho[24m symbols ``u'', ``g'', and ``o'' specify the user, group, and other
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     parts of the mode bits, respectively.  The [4mwho[24m symbol ``a'' is equivalent
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     to ``ugo''.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The [4mperm[24m symbols represent the portions of the mode bits as follows:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           r       The read bits.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           s       The set-user-ID-on-execution and set-group-ID-on-execution
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   bits.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           t       The sticky bit.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           w       The write bits.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           x       The execute/search bits.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           X       The execute/search bits if the file is a directory or any of
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   the execute/search bits are set in the original (unmodified)
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   mode.  Operations with the [4mperm[24m symbol ``X'' are only
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   meaningful in conjunction with the [4mop[24m symbol ``+'', and are
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   ignored in all other cases.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           u       The user permission bits in the original mode of the file.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           g       The group permission bits in the original mode of the file.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           o       The other permission bits in the original mode of the file.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The [4mop[24m symbols represent the operation performed, as follows:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     +     If no value is supplied for [4mperm[24m, the ``+'' operation has no effect.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           If no value is supplied for [4mwho[24m, each permission bit specified in
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           [4mperm[24m, for which the corresponding bit in the file mode creation mask
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           (see umask(2)) is clear, is set.  Otherwise, the mode bits
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           represented by the specified [4mwho[24m and [4mperm[24m values are set.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     -     If no value is supplied for [4mperm[24m, the ``-'' operation has no effect.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           If no value is supplied for [4mwho[24m, each permission bit specified in
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           [4mperm[24m, for which the corresponding bit in the file mode creation mask
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           is set, is cleared.  Otherwise, the mode bits represented by the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           specified [4mwho[24m and [4mperm[24m values are cleared.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     =     The mode bits specified by the [4mwho[24m value are cleared, or, if no [4mwho[24m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           value is specified, the owner, group and other mode bits are cleared.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           Then, if no value is supplied for [4mwho[24m, each permission bit specified
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           in [4mperm[24m, for which the corresponding bit in the file mode creation
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           mask (see umask(2)) is clear, is set.  Otherwise, the mode bits
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           represented by the specified [4mwho[24m and [4mperm[24m values are set.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     Each [4mclause[24m specifies one or more operations to be performed on the mode
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     bits, and each operation is applied to the mode bits in the order
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     specified.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     Operations upon the other permissions only (specified by the symbol ``o''
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     by itself), in combination with the [4mperm[24m symbols ``s'' or ``t'', are
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     ignored.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The ``w'' permission on directories will permit file creation, relocation,
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     and copy into that directory.  Files created within the directory itself
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     will inherit its group ID.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[1mEXAMPLES[0m [1mOF[0m [1mVALID[0m [1mMODES[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     644           make a file readable by anyone and writable by the owner
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   only.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     go-w          deny write permission to group and others.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     =rw,+X        set the read and write permissions to the usual defaults, but
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   retain any execute permissions that are currently set.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     +X            make a directory or file searchable/executable by everyone if
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   it is already searchable/executable by anyone.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     755
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     u=rwx,go=rx
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     u=rwx,go=u-w  make a file readable/executable by everyone and writable by
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   the owner only.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     go=           clear all mode bits for group and others.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     g=u-w         set the group bits equal to the user bits, but clear the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   group write bit.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[1mACL[0m [1mMANIPULATION[0m [1mOPTIONS[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     ACLs are manipulated using extensions to the symbolic mode grammar.  Each
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     file has one ACL, containing an ordered list of entries.  Each entry refers
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     to a user or group, and grants or denies a set of permissions.  In cases
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     where a user and a group exist with the same name, the user/group name can
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     be prefixed with "user:" or "group:" in order to specify the type of name.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     If the user or group name contains spaces you can use ':' as the delimiter
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     between name and permission.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The following permissions are applicable to all filesystem objects:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           delete  Delete the item.  Deletion may be granted by either this
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   permission on an object or the delete_child right on the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   containing directory.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           readattr
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Read an object's basic attributes.  This is implicitly
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   granted if the object can be looked up and not explicitly
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   denied.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           writeattr
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Write an object's basic attributes.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           readextattr
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Read extended attributes.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           writeextattr
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Write extended attributes.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           readsecurity
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Read an object's extended security information (ACL).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           writesecurity
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Write an object's security information (ownership, mode,
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   ACL).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           chown   Change an object's ownership.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The following permissions are applicable to directories:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           list    List entries.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           search  Look up files by name.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           add_file
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Add a file.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           add_subdirectory
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Add a subdirectory.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           delete_child
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Delete a contained object.  See the file delete permission
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   above.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The following permissions are applicable to non-directory filesystem
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     objects:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           read    Open for reading.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           write   Open for writing.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           append  Open for writing, but in a fashion that only allows writes
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   into areas of the file not previously written.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           execute
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Execute the file as a script or program.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     ACL inheritance is controlled with the following permissions words, which
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     may only be applied to directories:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           file_inherit
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Inherit to files.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           directory_inherit
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   Inherit to directories.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           limit_inherit
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   This flag is only relevant to entries inherited by
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   subdirectories; it causes the directory_inherit flag to be
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   cleared in the entry that is inherited, preventing further
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   nested subdirectories from also inheriting the entry.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K           only_inherit
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   The entry is inherited by created items but not considered
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                   when processing the ACL.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     The ACL manipulation options are as follows:
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m+a[0m      The +a mode parses a new ACL entry from the next argument on the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             commandline and inserts it into the canonical location in the ACL.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             If the supplied entry refers to an identity already listed, the two
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             entries are combined.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             [1mExamples[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod +a "admin allow write" file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: admin allow write
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod +a "guest deny read" file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: admin allow write
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod +a "admin allow delete" file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: admin allow write,delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod +a "User 1:allow:read" file
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: User 1 allow read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                3: admin allow write,delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             The +a mode strives to maintain correct canonical form for the ACL.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                              local deny
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                              local allow
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                              inherited deny
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                              inherited allow
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             By default, chmod adds entries to the top of the local deny and
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             local allow lists. Inherited entries are added by using the +ai
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             mode.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             [1mExamples[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: admin allow write,delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                3: juser inherited deny delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                4: admin inherited allow delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                5: backup inherited deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                6: admin inherited allow write-security
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod +ai "others allow read" file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: admin allow write,delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                3: juser inherited deny delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                4: others inherited allow read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                5: admin inherited allow delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                6: backup inherited deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                7: admin inherited allow write-security
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m+a#[0m     When a specific ordering is required, the exact location at which
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             an entry will be inserted is specified with the +a# mode.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             [1mExamples[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: admin allow write
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod +a# 2 "others deny read" file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: others deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                3: admin allow write
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             The +ai# mode may be used to insert inherited entries at a specific
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             location. Note that these modes allow non-canonical ACL ordering to
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             be constructed.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-a[0m      The -a mode is used to delete ACL entries. All entries exactly
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             matching the supplied entry will be deleted. If the entry lists a
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             subset of rights granted by an entry, only the rights listed are
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             removed. Entries may also be deleted by index using the -a# mode.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             [1mExamples[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: guest deny read
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                2: admin allow write,delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod -a# 1 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: admin allow write,delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod -a "admin allow write" file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: admin allow delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             Inheritance is not considered when processing the -a mode; rights
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             and entries will be removed regardless of their inherited state.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             If the user or group name contains spaces you can use ':' as the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             delimiter
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             [1mExample[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod +a "User 1:allow:read" file
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m=a#[0m     Individual entries are rewritten using the =a# mode.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             [1mExamples[0m
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: admin allow delete
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # chmod =a# 1 "admin allow write,chown"
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              # ls -le
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K              -rw-r--r--+ 1 juser  wheel  0 Apr 28 14:06 file1
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                owner: juser
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K                1: admin allow write,chown
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             This mode may not be used to add new entries.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-E[0m      Reads the ACL information from stdin, as a sequential list of ACEs,
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             separated by newlines.  If the information parses correctly, the
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             existing information is replaced.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-C[0m      Returns false if any of the named files have ACLs in non-canonical
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             order.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-i[0m      Removes the 'inherited' bit from all entries in the named file(s)
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K             ACLs.
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-I[0m      Removes all inherited entries from the named file(s) ACL(s).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K     [1m-N[0m      Removes the ACL from the named file(s).
:[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K
